‡¶®‡¶® ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡ßü‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá Compiled ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡ßü‡ßá‡¶ú‡•§

### ‚úÖ Compiled
compiled ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá machine language (binary code) ‡¶è convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü,  
‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### ‚úÖ How Scripting Language Run
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡ßü‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá compiled ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ,  
‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü interpreter  
(often part of the web server, like Apache or Nginx)‡•§  
‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßú‡ßá machine instructions ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

### ‚úÖ Web Host
‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶π‡ßã‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‚Äî ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã‡•§  
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶â ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§

### ‚úÖ Web Server
‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ü‡ßÅ‡¶≤ (tool) ‡¶¨‡¶æ software ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

### ‚úÖ XAMPP
xammp ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶ü‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶ú ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶ü‡ßÅ‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

```txt
X: Cross-platform (works on Windows, Linux, and macOS)
A: Apache (a web server that runs your website)
M: MySQL (a database that stores your data)
P: PHP (a programming language used to build web applications)
P: Perl (another programming language, though less commonly used today)
```

### ‚úÖ Case Sensitivity

**Case sensitivity** ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶° uppercase ‡¶¨‡¶æ lowercase ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

```txt
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® : Apple, apple ‚Äî ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®?
```

- **Case sensitive:** Apple, apple ‚Üí ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®
- **Not case sensitive:** Apple, apple ‚Üí ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á

> ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá PHP ‡¶§‡ßá user define classes ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç functions ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶Æ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§  
> ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®‡¶É `if`, `else`, `while`, `echo`

---

### ‚úÖ PHP Comment
php comment ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã execute ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§  
php comment ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶É

**Single line comment:**
```php
// single line comment
# another single line comment
```

**Multiple line comment:**
```php
/*
This is a multi-line comment
It spans across multiple lines
*/
```

## **********Variable*********

### variable
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá value assign ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá 
var_dump() function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ variable ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø .

### loosely typed language : 
PHP ‡¶π‡¶≤ loosely typed language. ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ declured ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßü‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ,
‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤‡•§ 
```example : $number = 5; [‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã interger ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ] .```
```$number = "PHP " [‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã string  ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ] .```
‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ java ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡ßü‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá vareable ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ declure ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ 
```example :  int number = 5; [‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá int ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá integer ‡¶ï‡¶•‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶á‡¶õ‡ßá ]```

### Types of Variable

### variable scope 
variable scope ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá variable ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ 
three main types of variable scope in PHP

### Local Scope
function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã variable ‡¶ï‡ßá  Local Scope ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá. 
‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ declured ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡¶á access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ 
‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ .

```
function myFunction() {
$name = "John";  // Local variable, only available inside this function
echo $name;
}
myFunction();  // Outputs: John
echo $name;    // Error: $name is not accessible outside the function
```

### Global Scope 
Global Scope ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã,‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã variable ‡¶ï‡ßá Global Scope ‡¶¨‡¶æ Global variable ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ 
‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ function ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ script ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü 

```<?php
$name = "Alice";  // Global variable

function myFunction() {
    echo $name;  // Error: Cannot access the global variable directly inside a function
}

myFunction();  // Will produce an error
?>
```
‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶ì‡¶á variable ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá global keyword use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã 

```<?php
$name = "Alice";  // Global variable

function myFunction() {
    global $name;  // Use the global keyword to access the global variable
    echo $name;    // Outputs: Alice
}

myFunction();
?>
```


### Static Scope 
‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ declured ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá,‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ì‡¶á function ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ì‡¶á ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ delete ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§ 
‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø variable ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá Static ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ì‡¶á ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶ü‡¶æ, 
function ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶ì‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ì‡¶á function ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ì‡¶á ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ì‡¶á ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá‡•§   
example
```    
<?php
function myFunction() {
    $count = 0;  // This is a regular variable
    $count++;
    echo $count;
}

myFunction();  // Outputs: 1
myFunction();  // Outputs: 1
myFunction();  // Outputs: 1
?>
```
**Simple Example without Static:
```
<?php
function myFunction() {
    $count = 0;  // This is a regular variable
    $count++;
    echo $count;
}

myFunction();  // Outputs: 1
myFunction();  // Outputs: 1
myFunction();  // Outputs: 1
?>
```
**Example with Static:  
```
?php
function myFunction() {
    static $count = 0;  // This is a static variable
    $count++;
    echo $count;
}

myFunction();  // Outputs: 1
myFunction();  // Outputs: 2
myFunction();  // Outputs: 3
?>
```

## Echo/Print

echo ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç print ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶Ü‡¶â‡¶ü‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶ü show ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ 

### echo 
echo ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶≤‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶â‡¶ü‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶ü ‡¶∂‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ 
echo print ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ 

### print 
print ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡ßß ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ expressions ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§  
example 

```
<?php
if (print("Hello")) {
    echo " - The print function returned 1, so this message is shown.";
}
?>
```
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá print("Hello") ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ç hellow ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç  1 ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø  ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü 1 ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ 
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡ßß ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ condtion ‡¶ü‡¶æ true . ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ condition ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ü‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßÅ excute ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü 1 ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ 
‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ expressions ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ 
   
### why 1 is True
php ‡¶§‡ßá 1 ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü true ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞  ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç 0 false ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ 
    example 
```
<?php
if (1) {
    echo "This will be executed because 1 is true.";
}

if (0) {
    echo "This will NOT be executed because 0 is false.";
}
?>   
```

### expressions 
expressions ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã value ,variable ,operator and function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ combination ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡ßÄ  ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤ value ) .

```example : $x = 5 + 3;  // "5 + 3" is an expression that evaluates to 8 ```

Expression with Variables
```
$a = 5;
$b = 3;
$result = $a * $b;  // "$a * $b" is an expression that evaluates to 15
```

Expression with Condition

```
if (10 > 5) {
    echo "Yes";  // "10 > 5" is an expression that evaluates to true
}
```
Function Call as Expression:
```$length = strlen("Hello");  // "strlen('Hello')" is an expression that evaluates to 5```

## PHP Data Types

### Data Type
 Data type ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü ,‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞  type of data (value ) hold ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ 

### PHP has 8 main data types:

### String 
String ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ sequence of characters (‡¶Ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Æ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∏‡•§‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ character ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞  ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ character ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ 
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® "CAT" ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá C A ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç T ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡ßü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶á‡¶®‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ) 
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ Double Quotes (") ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Single Quotes (') ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§   
Characters: Letters (like A, B, C), digits (like 1, 2, 3), and symbols (like @, #, !).   
‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø single quotes (') or double quotes (") ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§  

### Integer
Integer ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßá (Negativ ‡¶è‡¶®‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶™‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≠ )‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá decimal ‡¶®‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞ ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ‡•§  

### Float (or Double)
Float (or Double) ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ decimal ‡¶®‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶ø‡•§ 

### Boolean 
Boolean ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ data Type ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ true ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç false ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶ü‡¶æ state ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
true : (‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã something are correct or  exit ).
False : (‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã  something is incorrect or does not exist).

### When is Boolean Used?
Boolean ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü Conditional Statements and Logical and comparison Operations ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ 
Conditional Statements : (like if, else) ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ true ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç false ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ  block ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ü‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶®  run hobe ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡•§ 
‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø condtion true ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® run ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá other wise ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ 
Logical and comparison Operations (like &&, || , > ,<) to combine or test multiple conditions.

 besic example 

 ```
<?php
$is_raining = true;   // This is a boolean value representing 'true'
$is_sunny = false;    // This is a boolean value representing 'false'

if ($is_raining) {
    echo "Take an umbrella!";  // This will run because $is_raining is true
}

if (!$is_sunny) {
    echo "It's not sunny outside.";  // This will run because $is_sunny is false
}
?>
```

Comparisons example

```
 <?php
$a = 10;
$b = 5;

$is_greater = $a > $b;  // Comparison: 10 is greater than 5, so $is_greater is true
echo $is_greater;       // Outputs: 1 (because true is displayed as 1 in PHP)

$is_equal = $a == $b;   // Comparison: 10 is not equal to 5, so $is_equal is false
echo $is_equal;         // Outputs nothing (because false is displayed as empty in PHP)
?>
```

### Type Casting 
Type Casting ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ process ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá value ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ data type ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ data type convert ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§    
PHP ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ automatically Booleans data ‡¶ï‡¶®‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá example ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã : 

0 (integer zero) and 0.0 (float zero) are false.
Empty strings (""), empty arrays ([]), and null are false.
All other values (non-zero numbers, non-empty strings, non-empty arrays) are true.

```
<?php
$value1 = 0;         // 0 is false
$value2 = "Hello";   // Non-empty string is true

if ($value1) {
    echo "This is true!";
} else {
    echo "This is false!";  // Outputs this because 0 is false
}

if ($value2) {
    echo "This is true!";  // Outputs this because non-empty strings are true
}
?>
```

### Array 
Array ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá  multiple ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ assign ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá index ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§             
example 

```
<?php
$fruits = array("Apple", "Banana", "Orange");  // This is an array
echo $fruits[0];  // Outputs: Apple (first item in the array)
?>
```

### Object
Object ‡¶π‡¶≤ instance of class . ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá object ‡¶π‡¶≤ class ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶¨ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡•§ 
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® car ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ class ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¨‡¶æ instance ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Toyota .   
class : class ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü plan . ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® (car ,‡¶è‡¶∞ color ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ,brand ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶® ) .
object : object ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶ê ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶æ class  ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ real ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® (car ‡¶è‡¶∞ color ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶° ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá , ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶ü‡¶æ Toyota ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ) .
‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã multiple  ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¨‡¶æ object ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶∏ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡•§ 

```
class Car {
    public $color;
    public $model;
}

// Creating an instance of the Car class
$myCar = new Car();  // This is an instance (or object) of the Car class
$myCar->color = "Blue";
$myCar->model = "Toyota";

$myNewCar = new Car();  // multiple object 
$myNewCar->color = "red";
$myNewCar->model = "Tesla";
```

### NULL
NULL ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá  ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ special  ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ represents ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá no-value ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ empty ‡•§ 
‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡ßá null ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ê ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶ü‡¶æ empty ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§
‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá Declaring without a value.‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶•‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá 

$car;
$car2 = NULL;
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ declured ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶á‡•§ 
‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßÄ‡ßü‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ special null ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ assign ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶• ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ì ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§  ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á‡•§ 

$car;
PHP ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá $car  ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá , ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ initialized variable ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶Ü‡¶ö‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ 
initialized variable ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã variable ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá intial ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ (‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶•‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ  assign ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ )  
assign ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶ï‡¶•‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ $car  ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ exit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ PHP ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã memory allocation ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé memory ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ 

$car2 = NULL
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá $car2 variable  ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ special ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ declured ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ  initialized ‡¶ì ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá  ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç memory allocation ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Æ‡•§ 

### Resource 
Resource ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá PHP ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ special ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ external resource ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ 
external resource ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá PHP Program ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã data ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ service, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá PHP program ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá accessed ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ 
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® Databases,file ,API .  
example 
```
$connection = mysqli_connect("localhost", "username", "password", "database");
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá $connection ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ variable ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá database  ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§  
```

## PHP Strings Details

‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ string ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ string ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶∏ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ö‡ßã‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßã‡•§ 
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø string ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ  ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ  Double Quotes (") ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Single Quotes (') ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ 
‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶á Double Quotes (") ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Single Quotes (') ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ 

Double Quotes : 
                     
‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Double Quotes ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§ 
‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶Ü‡¶ö‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶á‡¶Ç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶∂ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá (interpolated).  
‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ 
```
$name = "John";
echo "Hello, $name!"; // Outputs: Hello, John!
```
‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï escape sequences ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßã‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ (escape sequences ‡¶π‡¶≤ combination  of special character) .
            
performance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Single Quotes ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá slow  ‡•§            
Double Quotes ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ single  Quotes ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ 
```
echo "She said, 'Hello!' "; 
```

Single Quotes (') 
                     
‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶Ü‡¶ö‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ sequence characters ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® :
```
$name = "John";
echo 'Hello, $name!';  // Outputs: Hello, $name!
```
            
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá $name ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ  ‡¶è‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶ì‡¶á ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ sequence characters ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ 
            
*‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø escape sequences ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßã‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ 
\' to include a single quote (like in It's),
\\ to include a backslash.
            
performance ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø Double Quotes ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá faster ‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá  interpolation ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ  ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç escape sequences ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßã‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ 
Single Quotes ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ Double Quotes ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ 
```
echo 'She said, "Hello!"'; 
```
‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßá  '.' ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ concate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§   

## PHP Constants
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ assign ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ 
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® 
```
$name = "‡¶ñ‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá "; 
```
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá $name ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ string ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶§‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®‡¶ø Constant ‡¶ì ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ special variable ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ assign ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ 
‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá Constant ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç variable ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡•§ 

 ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßá define() ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ  const ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ 
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ 
```
 define("SITE_NAME", "MyWebsite");
 ```
‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ changed or redefined ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡•§ 
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ 
```
define("PI", 3.14159); 
// Trying to change the value
PI = 3.9; // Error: Cannot reassign a value to a constant
```
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ PI ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶á‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶û‡ßç‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ 
```
define("GREETING", "Hello, World!"); // Define the constant GREETING
define("GREETING", "Hi, World!"); // Error: GREETING has already been defined
```
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ GREETING define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á‡•§ 
‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ uppercase letters ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ 
‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶∞ $ sign ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ 
PHP ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï magic constant ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶á predefine ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá details ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ 
‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï : https://www.w3schools.com/php/php_magic_constants.asp

 ## PHP Operators
PHP ‡¶§‡ßá Operators ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ  symbol ‡¶¨‡¶æ keyword (keyword ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá reserve keyword ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§  
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® if ,else ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø  ). ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü variable‡¶¨‡¶æ value ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞‡•§ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ action  ‡¶ò‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ 
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá action ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® : ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ,comapare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ,‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§  

```
Arithmetic operators (+,  -,  *,  /,  %)
Assignment operators (=, += , -=, *= , /= , %=)
Comparison operators (== , === , < ,> ,!= , <= ,>= ,)
Increment/Decrement operators (++$x , $x++ ,--$x , $x--)
Logical operators(&& , ‡•§‡•§ ,!)
String operators (. use to concate string )
Array operators (+ , == , === , != ,)
Conditional assignment operators (Ternary Operator ?:  ,  Null Coalescing Operator ?? )
Null coalescing operator : ‡¶è‡¶á operator ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ 
```

## PHP if Statements
PHP IF  statement ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ condtion ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ condtion ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® true ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§  
‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ì‡¶á condition ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ code ‡¶ü‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßÅ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶® ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ 
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ 
```
if (condition) {
    // Code to run if the condition is true
}
```
‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ternary ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶•‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ ternary operator ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá if statement ‡¶è‡¶∞  short form ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá shorthand if ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
 ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ 
``` 
$variable = (condition) ? value_if_true : value_if_false;

$age = 20;
$status = ($age >= 18) ? "adult" : "minor";
echo $status; // Outputs: adult  
```
‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï condition ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ if elseif ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ switch Statement ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶ì multiple condition check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá switch Statement ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡•§

‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ :
```
$fruit = "apple";
switch ($fruit) {
    case "banana":
        echo "This is a banana.";
        break;
    case "apple":
        echo "This is an apple.";
        break;
    case "orange":
        echo "This is an orange.";
        break;
    default:
        echo "Unknown fruit.";
}
```

## PHP Loop

Loop ‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ connditional statement .‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ‡ßü : ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü block ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ excute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ) 
‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶æ condtion ‡¶ü‡¶æ false ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ php ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ loop ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá , while Loop,do-while Loop,for Loop,foreach Loop

while Loop 

```
$count = 1;
while ($count <= 5) {
    echo "Count is: $count <br>";
    $count++; // Increases $count by 1 each time
}
```

do-while Loop 

```
$count = 1;
do {
    echo "Count is: $count <br>";
    $count++;
} while ($count <= 5);
```
‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá while Loop ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç do-while Loop ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã while Loop ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá condition  check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ,
‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶™‡¶∞  condtion true ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ü‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßÅ excute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ 
‡¶ì‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá  do-while Loop ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° excute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá then condition check ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ 

for Loop
```
for ($i = 1; $i <= 5; $i++) {
    echo "Number: $i <br>";
}
```

Step-by-Step Execution
Let's go through each iteration to see what happens.

First Iteration:

Initialization: $i = 1
Condition: $i <= 5 (true, since 1 <= 5)
Execute Code: echo "Number: 1 <br>"; // Output: Number: 1
Increment: $i++ makes $i = 2
Second Iteration:

Condition: $i <= 5 (true, since 2 <= 5)
Execute Code: echo "Number: 2 <br>"; // Output: Number: 2
Increment: $i++ makes $i = 3
Third Iteration:

Condition: $i <= 5 (true, since 3 <= 5)
Execute Code: echo "Number: 3 <br>"; // Output: Number: 3
Increment: $i++ makes $i = 4
Fourth Iteration:

Condition: $i <= 5 (true, since 4 <= 5)
Execute Code: echo "Number: 4 <br>"; // Output: Number: 4
Increment: $i++ makes $i = 5
Fifth Iteration:

Condition: $i <= 5 (true, since 5 <= 5)
Execute Code: echo "Number: 5 <br>"; // Output: Number: 5
Increment: $i++ makes $i = 6
Sixth Iteration:

Condition: $i <= 5 (false, since 6 > 5)
Since the condition is now false, the loop stops, and PHP moves on to the next part of the code.

foreach Loop : foreach Loop ‡¶ü‡¶æ specially array ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü     
Break Statement : Break Statement ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã loop ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ‡ßé‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá exit ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø,
‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ì ‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶™ ‡¶è‡¶∞ condition true . ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßã ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

```
$count = 1;
while ($count <= 10) {
    echo "Count is: $count <br>";
    if ($count == 5) {
        break; // Stop the loop when $count is 5
    }
    $count++;
}
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá while loop ‡¶ü‡¶æ  $count  ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ , ‡ßß‡ß¶ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®  ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶§‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶® ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ü‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßÅ excute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶•‡¶æ‡•§ 
‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ loop ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ  condition use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ì‡¶á condition true ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® break statement  ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá exit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá ,
‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ì loop ‡¶è‡¶∞ condition ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®‡ßã true ‡•§‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï statement ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú  

### Continue 
continue statement ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü  ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ loop ( ‡¶ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞ ) ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡•§
‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ì‡¶á loop (‡¶ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞) ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶™ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶™ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ continue ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ 
‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ break ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã loop ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá exit ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡•§ 

```
for ($i = 1; $i <= 5; $i++) {
    if ($i == 3) {
        continue; // $i = 3 ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á iteration (‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞ ) ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶™ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá
    }
    echo "Number: $i <br>";
}
```
‡¶Ü‡¶â‡¶ü‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶ü 
Number: 1
Number: 2
Number: 4
Number: 5
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® $i  = 3 ‡¶è‡¶á condition ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶ì‡¶á ‡¶ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ loop ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá skip ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ ‡¶Ø‡ßá loop ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶ê‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá Continue ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ 
[ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡•§ $i = 1; $i <= 5; $i++ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡ß´ ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ö‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ loop ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ condition ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá $i <= 5; ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá $i ‡¶è‡¶∞ 5 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßú ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ 
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø loop ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü block ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ excute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶æ condtion ‡¶ü‡¶æ false ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§  ]

## PHP Function

php function ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá code ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü block ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ 

[code ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ instructions (‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ) ‡¶¨‡¶æ command ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã programming language ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ,
 ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ì‡¶á instructions ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá (excution ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá )‡•§
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø code ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü programming ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡ßü‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï single ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® code ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü computer ‡¶ï‡ßá  ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞ , 
‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® compute ‡¶ì‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§ 
‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü‡¶ï‡¶•‡¶æ computer ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá commnucation ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° [ (programming ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡ßü‡ßá‡¶ú‡ßá) . 
‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶≤‡ßá programming language ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™ ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°].

example

```
<?php
echo "Hello, World!";
?>
```
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° instructions ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá computer ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø Hello, World! ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü ‡¶ü‡¶æ screen ‡¶∂‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§ 

function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ 

Reusability (‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ )
Organization (‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶ó‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶§ )
Maintainability (‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶æ , ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡ßÅ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶∏ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ function 
‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá , ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶ì‡¶á function ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶®‡¶ø ,‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶á function call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§)

‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ (function):

```
<?php
function sayHello() {
    echo "Hello, World!";
}

// Calling the function
sayHello(); // Outputs: Hello, World!
?>
```
function ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶Æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§  function ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡ßá function ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ 
sayHello ‡¶π‡¶≤ function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá function ‡¶ï‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡•§ function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ code ‡¶ï‡ßá exction ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá call ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§ 
‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ call ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ  exction ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ 

Parameters: Inputs to make functions flexible

```
function greet($name) {
    echo "Hello, $name!";
}
greet("Alice");
```
Return Values: Get results back from functions.  

```
function add($a, $b) {
    return $a + $b;
}
$sum = add(5, 3);
```
                    
Default Parameters: Provide default values for parameters

```
function greet($name = "Guest") {
    echo "Hello, $name!";
}
```

PHP ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ function ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ 

User-Defined Functions : ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã User ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã function ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá User-Defined Functions ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ 
                                 
‡¶â‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶®

```
<?php
function greet() {
    echo "Hello, World!";
}
greet(); 
?>
```

Built-in Functions : Built-in Functions ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá define ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡ßÄ  ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ function ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶¨‡¶æ modification ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ 
‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§php ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï Built-in Functions ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø 
‡¶â‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶®

```
echo round(4.6); // Outputs: 5
round ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Built-in Functions ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü neares integer velue ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü  
```

Anonymous Functions (Closures) : Anonymous Functions ‡¶ï‡ßá Closures function ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ 
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü  inline functions or assigned to variables ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶ø inline functions ‡¶ï‡¶ø   
inline functions ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü function ‡¶¨‡¶æ  temporary functions ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá , 
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ immediately ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞  ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ì‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® plan ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ reuse ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßã ‡•§ 

example:
Inline function to square a number

```
$square = function($number) {
    return $number * $number;
};
echo $square(4); // Output: 16
```

explain: Here, $square(4) means you are calling the anonymous function stored in $square and 
passing 4 as the value for the parameter $number. ["function is stored," it means that the function is assigned to a variable.]   


assigned to variables ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ú‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ, ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶≤ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡•§ 
‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® $x = "‡ßß‡ß¶";
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá $x ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡ßß‡ß¶ ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡•§ 
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Anonymous Functions ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶â ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§     
finally ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø  ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç immediately ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ use ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ Anonymous Functions ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ò‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã function ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ 
‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° short ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§     
                                        
Anonymous Functions ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∞‡¶á‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ Local Scope . Scope ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ö‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ,‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶™ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá accessible 
area . ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶ó‡¶æ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ Local Scope ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá declured ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ ‡¶ê‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ 
‡¶â‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶® ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ 

```
$name = "Alice";
$sayHello = function() use ($name) { // Captures $name from outside
    echo "Hello, $name";
};
$sayHello(); // Output: Hello, Alice
```


‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá $name ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ variable ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßá declured ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá  function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ error ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶¨‡ßá . 
‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßá function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤  access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Anonymous Functions  "use " ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶° ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá 
function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Æ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∏‡•§  

Arrow function: arrow function ‡¶ì Anonymous Function ‡¶è‡¶∞  ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ inline functions,‡¶è‡¶á function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá 
‡¶®‡¶æ ,‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶ì variable assign ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡ßã function ‡¶á ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü task ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ 
‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ arrow function ‡¶è‡¶∞‡•§ 

```
<?php
$c = 0; // outer scope variable
$sum = fn($a, $b) => $a + $b + $c;
echo $sum(5, 10); // Output: 15  
php?> 
```

‡¶´‡ßÄ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞                                    Arrow function                           

1.Syntax                              fn  keyword ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ 
2.Return                              ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá return ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá result return ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ 

3.Outer Scope Variables               outer scope variable access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã keyword ‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶ü‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶á access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ 
4.Introduced in PHP                   PHP 7.4
5.code cmplexcity                     Can not handle multiple lines of code




‡¶´‡ßÄ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞                                    Anonymous Function                            

1.Syntax                              function  keyword ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§  
2.Return                              function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ result ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø return  ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§                 

3.Outer Scope Variables               outer scope variable access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø use keyword ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü
4.Introduced in PHP                   PHP 5.3
5.code cmplexcity                     Can  handle multiple lines of code


Recursive Functions (call) :Recursive Functions  ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá Recursive Call ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ base case (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶ô‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶¨‡ßá,‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ‡•§  ) 
‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã recursive case (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá recursion ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá) 

 ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã 

```
function countdown($number) {
if ($number <= 0) { // Base case
    return;
}
echo $number . "\n"; // Print the current number
countdown($number - 1); // Recursive call
}

countdown(5);
```

## Array
Array ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá  multiple ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ assign ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá index ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ 
example

```
<?php
$fruits = array("Apple", "Banana", "Orange");  // This is an array
echo $fruits[0];  // Outputs: Apple (first item in the array)
?>
```

Type of Array:

Indexed Arrays: Arrays with numeric keys (starting from 0).
Associative Arrays: Arrays with custom string keys.
Multidimensional Arrays: Arrays containing other arrays.


Indexed Arrays : Indexed Arrays  ‡¶§‡ßá  integer key ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ auto generate ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø manually assign ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ 
Example: 

```
<?php
$fruits = ["apple", "banana", "orange"]; // Indexed array

echo $fruits[0]; // Outputs: apple
echo $fruits[1]; 
?>
```

Associative Arrays : Associative Arrays ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ string key ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ,‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá integer key ‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶á‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡ßü ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

```
$associativeArray = [
"name" => "Alice", // String key
42 => "Meaning of life", // Integer key
"city" => "Paris"
    ];
echo $associativeArray["name"]; // Outputs: Alice
echo $associativeArray[42];  
?>
```

               
main ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Indexed Arrays ‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡ßü ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü integer ,‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ auto genarate .‡¶ì‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá Associative Arrays key string ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ integer .( ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá fully customize )
USES : Indexed Arrays ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ  sequential data (like a list or collection) store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø. 
‡¶Ü‡¶∞ Associative Arrays ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü meaningful keys ‡¶∏‡¶π ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ store ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ 
Key  : ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ array ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ multiple ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶ø ,‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶π‡ßá‡¶§‡ßÅ spacific ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶á ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ Key ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶®‡ßç‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã Key .   

Multidimensional arrays : Multidimensional arrays ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ array ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá array ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá‡•§ 
‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø array ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤  ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá  ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ assign ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ 
‡¶Ü‡¶∞ Multidimensional arrays ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ê ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá array assign ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá example ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡•§ 

Types of Multidimensional Arrays
Two-Dimensional Array:  (array ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ array )    
Three-Dimensional Array: (array ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ two-dimensional array) 
N-Dimensional Array:  (Arrays with more nested levels)


Two-Dimensional Array : Two-Dimensional Array ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ multiple array , ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶æ row ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç column ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶ö‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡•§ 

```
$products = [   ["Laptop", 1200, 5],["Smartphone", 800, 10],["Tablet", 400, 7]   ];
```

               
‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ Two-Dimensional Array . ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá $products ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ main array ,‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã assign  ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ì ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ array . 
‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá  row ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç column ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶ö‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá main Array ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá row ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá array ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá column . ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶É 
               
```               
$products = [   

["Laptop",        1200,                5],             =======> first row (0 index)
    ‡•§                ‡•§                  ‡•§
    ‡•§                ‡•§                  ‡•§
(1r  ,1c  )     (1r ,2c )       (1r ,3c )
(0 index)      (1 index)     (3 index)



["Smartphone",         800,          10],    =======> second  row (1 index)

    ‡•§                    ‡•§                  ‡•§
    ‡•§                    ‡•§                  ‡•§
(2r  ,1c  )         (2r ,2c )       (2r ,3c )

(0 index)           (1 index)     (3 index)


["Tablet",        400,             7]                 =======> third  row (2 index)

    ‡•§                ‡•§               ‡•§
    ‡•§                ‡•§               ‡•§
(3r  ,1c  )     (3r ,2c )       (3r ,3c )
(0 index)      (1 index)     (3 index)

];
```

Three-Dimensional (3D) Array : Three-Dimensional  Array ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶™‡¶≤ array .‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá main array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ 
two-dimensional array . ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá Associative Arrays ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ 

```
    $school = [
    
        "Class 1" => [
            ["Rasel", "A+"],
            ["Rahim", "B"]
    
        ],
    
        "Class 2" => [
            ["Karim", "A"],
            ["Jamal", "C"]
    
        ]
    ];

    ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶® ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤ 

    $school = [
    
    [
        ["Rasel", "A+"],
        ["Rahim", "B"]

    ],

    [
        ["Karim", "A"],
        ["Jamal", "C"]

    ]
];
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá $school ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ main array ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá two dimension array .

N-Dimensional Array :  N-Dimensional array ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤  main array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá (‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ array ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã  index ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡ß¶,‡ßß‡•§ ‡¶ì‡¶á ‡ß¶ index ‡¶Ø‡¶§ ‡¶§‡¶§ array ) ‡¶Ø‡¶§ ‡¶§‡¶§ array .‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡•§ 

```
    $universe = [
    [
        [
            ["Life Exists", "Oxygen Available"]
        ]
    ],

[
    [
        ["Life not Exists", "Oxygen not Available"]
    ]
    ]
]
```
Behind the seen in Array (how its work): 
‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßã, PHP ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø RAM-‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® (value) ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶æ‡ßü (Memory Address) ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ CPU ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

‡¶ï‡ßÄ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá PHP ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá RAM-‡¶è ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá?

1Ô∏è‚É£ ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® $array = ["Apple", "Banana", "Mango"]; ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßã, PHP ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø RAM-‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
2Ô∏è‚É£ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Memory Address ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®:

```
Index	Value	Memory Address (RAM)
0	Apple	        0x100
1	Banana	        0x104
2	Mango	        0x108
3Ô∏è‚É£ ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶ø echo $array[1]; ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßã, PHP RAM ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 0x104 ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶°‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá "Banana" ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡ßá‡•§
```

## superglobal variables
        
1.$_GET ‚Äì URL ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ
$_GET ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ URL-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ : ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßã, ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞ URL ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‚Äì https://example.com?name=Rasel&age=25
‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶®, PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ $_GET ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‚Äì

```
<?php
echo "‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ: " . $_GET['name'] . "<br>";
echo "‡¶¨‡ßü‡¶∏: " . $_GET['age'];
?>
```
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞: ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® $_GET ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§        

2.‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞: $_POST ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶æ URL-‡¶è ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡ßã, ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶ó‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶´‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‚Äì    

```
<form action="process.php" method="POST">
    ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶Æ: <input type="text" name="username"><br>
    ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶°: <input type="password" name="password"><br>
    <input type="submit" value="‡¶≤‡¶ó‡¶á‡¶®">
</form>
```

‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßã ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶≤‡ßá 

```

echo "‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶°: " . $_POST['password'];
?>
```

‡¶Ü‡¶â‡¶ü‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶ü (‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ 'Rasel' ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç '1234' ‡¶¶‡ßá‡ßü)

3.$_REQUEST ‚Äì GET ‡¶ì POST ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá     
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:

‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞: ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ $_GET ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶ø $_POST ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® $_REQUEST ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§


4.$_FILES ‚Äì ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡ßü 

5.$_SERVER ‚Äì ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá  ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§  
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ :

‡¶§‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞ IP: 192.168.1.1  
‡¶§‡ßã‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞: Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64)
        
6.$_ENV ‚Äì ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶®‡¶≠‡¶æ‡ßü‡¶∞‡¶®‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ
‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ :

‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞: ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§


7.$_GLOBALS ‚Äì  ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü , ‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø

```

    echo "‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ: " . $GLOBALS['name'];

```    
‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞: ‡¶Ø‡¶ñ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á‡•§    

8.$_SESSION ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç $_COOKIE ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∏ ‡¶®‡ßü, ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

### $_SESSION 

1.‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶°‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ 
2.‡¶Ø‡¶§‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ß ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßÅ‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø session_destroy() ‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ,‡¶§‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶™‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá?
3.‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶¶, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§  $_SESSION ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßã‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá (RAM) ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
4.‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ /tmp/sess_abc123 ‡¶è‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶´‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
5.$_SESSION ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü
